the event target chain.\n   *       It is up to the Pre/PostHandleEvent implementation to decide how to\n   *       use these bits.\n   *\n   * @note Using uint16_t because that is used also in EventTargetChainItem.\n   */\n  uint16_t mItemFlags;\n\n  /**\n   * Data for items in the event target chain.\n   * Set in GetEventTargetParent() and used in PostHandleEvent().\n   *\n   * @note This data is different for each item in the event target chain.\n   *       It is up to the Pre/PostHandleEvent implementation to decide how to\n   *       use this.\n   */\n  nsCOMPtr<nsISupports> mItemData;\n};\n\nclass MOZ_STACK_CLASS EventChainPreVisitor final : public EventChainVisitor {\n public:\n  MOZ_CAN_RUN_SCRIPT\n  EventChainPreVisitor(nsPresContext* aPresContext, WidgetEvent* mParentTarget = aParentTarget;\n    if (mParentTarget) {\n      mParentIsChromeHandler = aIsChromeHandler;\n    }\n  }\n\n  void IgnoreCurrentTargetBecauseOfShadowDOMRetargeting();\n\n  /**\n   * (If it does call preventDefault, we should ignore it).\n  bool mPassive : 1;\n  // If mOnce is true, the listener will be removed from the manager before it\n  // is invoked, so that it would only be invoked once.\n  bool mOnce : 1;\n\n  EventListenerFlags()\n      : mListenerIsJSListener(false),\n        mCapture(false),\n        mInSystemGroup(false),\n        mAllowUntrustedEvents(false),\n        mPassive(false),\n        mOnce(false) {}\n\n  bool EqualsForAddition(const EventListenerFlags& aOther) const {\n    return (mCapture == aOther.mCapture &&\n            mInSystemGroup == aOther.mInSystemGroup &&\n            mListenerIsJSListener == aOther.mListenerIsJSListener &&\n            mAllowUntrustedEvents == aOther.mAllowUntrustedEvents);\n    // Don't compare mPassive or mOnce\n  }\n\n  bool EqualsForRemoval(const EventListenerFlags& aOther) const {\n    return (mCapture == aOther.mCapture &&\n            mInSystemGroup == aOther.mInSystemGroup &&\n            mListenerIsJSListener == aOther.mListenerIsJSListener);\n    // Don't compare mAllowUntrustedEvents, mPassive, or mOnce\n  }\n};\n\ninline EventListenerFlags TrustedEventsAtBubble() {\n  EventListenerFlags flags;\n  return flags;\n}\n\ninline EventListenerFlags TrustedEventsAtCapture() {\n  EventListenerFlags flags;\n  flags.mCapture = true;\n  return flags;","numLines":100,"startLine":1,"totalLines":767}}}

implemented in several key C++ modules:\\n\\n### 1. Event Creation\\n**Files**: `widget/BasicEvents.h`, `dom/events/Event.cpp`, `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`\\n\\n- **WidgetEvent** (`widget/BasicEvents.h`): Base class for all events, contains event properties like `mMessage`, `mTarget`, `mRelatedTarget`, and flags for `mBubbles`, `mCancelable`, `mIsTrusted`, etc.\\n- **Event** (`dom/events/Event.cpp`): DOM Event object wrapping the internal WidgetEvent\\n- **EventDispatcher::CreateEvent** (`dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`, line ~1380): Creates DOM Event objects from WidgetEvents\\n\\n### 2. Event Target Identification\\n**Files**: `dom/events/EventTarget.h`, `dom/events/EventTarget.cpp`, `dom/events/EventDispatcher.h`\\n\\n- **EventTarget** (`dom/events/EventTarget.h`): Abstract base class for all event targets (Elements, Windows, XMLHttpRequest, etc.)\\n- **EventTarget::AddEventListener** (`dom/events/EventTarget.cpp`): Registers event listeners\\n- **EventChainPreVisitor** and **EventChainPostVisitor** (`dom/events/EventDispatcher.h`): Used to traverse and build the event target chain\\n\\n### 3. Event Target Chain Construction\\n**File**: `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`\\n\\n- **EventDispatcher::Dispatch** (line ~869): Entry point for event dispatch. Creates the event target chain by:\\n  1. Setting up the initial target and original target\\n  2. Calling `GetEventTargetParent` on each target to build the chain\\n  3. Handling event retargeting for Shadow DOM\\n  4. Creating `EventTargetChainItem` objects for each target in the chain\\n\\n- **EventTargetChainItem** (line ~125): Represents a single item in the event target chain, storing:\\n  - The event target\\n  - Flags for capture/bubble phases\\n  - Retargeting information for Shadow DOM\\n  - Reference to the event listener manager\\n\\n### 4. Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal\\n**File**: `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`\\n\\n- **EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain** (line ~491): Core dispatch logic implementing W3C event dispatch algorithm:\\n  - **Capture Phase**: Iterates from root to target, backwards through the chain (line ~520)\\n  - **Target Phase**: Dispatches to the target itself (line ~588-606)\\n  - **Bubble Phase**: Iterates from target back to root, forwards through the chain (line ~614)\\n  - **System Group Dispatch**: Re-dispatches in system group for chrome/default handling (line ~651-687)\\n\\n- Sets event flags: `mInCapturePhase`, `mInBubblingPhase`, `mInTargetPhase`, `mInSystemGroup` to indicate current phase\\n\\n### 5. Default Action Execution\\n**Files**: `dom/events/EventStateManager.h`, `dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp`\\n\\n- **EventStateManager::PostHandleEvent** (line ~3977): Executes default actions\\n  - Called after the system group dispatch\\n  - Performs browser default behaviors (navigate on link click, submit forms, etc.)\\n  - Only executes if `preventDefault()` was not called\\n  - Handles retargeted events properly\\n\\n### 7.
